		<div class="g_bubble desc">
<b>Kugimiya Rie</b> was born May 30, 1979 in Osaka, Japan and brought up in Kumamoto. She is a voice actress currently affiliated with <a href="http://anidb.net/cr1455">I'm Enterprise</a>.<br><br>Kugimiya is most known for the roles of <a href="http://anidb.net/ch5908">Alphonse Elric</a> in <a href="http://anidb.net/a979">Fullmetal Alchemist</a>, <a href="http://anidb.net/ch26">Shana</a> in <a href="http://anidb.net/a3408">Shakugan no Shana</a>, <a href="http://anidb.net/ch1164">Kagura</a> in <a href="http://anidb.net/a3468">Gintama</a> and more recently, <a href="http://anidb.net/ch1009">Aisaka Taiga</a> in <a href="http://anidb.net/a5909">Toradora!</a>. She is typecasted to tsundere roles due to her voicing of tsundere characters <a href="http://anidb.net/ch528">Nagi</a> (<a href="http://anidb.net/a4917">Hayate no Gotoku!</a>), <a href="http://anidb.net/ch26">Shana</a> (<a href="http://anidb.net/a3408">Shakugan no Shana</a>) and <a href="http://anidb.net/ch306">Louise</a> (<a href="http://anidb.net/a4146">Zero no Tsukaima</a>), all of whose anime aired around the same time. Due to her popularity in such roles, some of her fans have named her as the <a href="http://anidb.net/l90">Queen of Tsundere</a>.<br><br>She was nominated for Best Actress in Leading Role in the first Seiyu Awards for the role of <a href="http://anidb.net/ch306">Louise</a> in <a href="http://anidb.net/a4146">Zero no Tsukaima</a>, and jointly won Best Actress in a Supporting Role with <a href="http://anidb.net/cr180">Saiga Mitsuki</a> at the second Seiyu Awards. Kugimiya won Best Actress in the third seiyu awards for the role of <a href="http://anidb.net/ch1009">Aisaka Taiga</a> in <a href="http://anidb.net/a5909">Toradora!</a>.
		</div>
